<p style="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Zion
Oil and Gas, Inc., a Delaware corporation, which has an active petroleum exploration operation onshore Israel in the Megiddo-Jezreel
area,<span style="color: #26282A; background-color: white">&#160;announces the approval on September 14, 2023 of a new Megiddo Valleys
License 434, allowing for ongoing oil and gas exploration on approximately 75,000 acres or 302 square kilometers. The Exploration License
434 will be valid for three years until September 13, 2026 with four 1-year extensions for a total of seven years until September 13,
2030.</span></span></p>

<p style="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Zion
plans to start re-completion operations on the Megiddo-Jezreel #1 well (MJ-01) as soon as possible. Zion is deploying new technologies,
focusing on new stimulation methods for MJ-01, and aiming to unlock potential hydrocarbon flows in several identified key zones. Zion
has already procured service contractors and ancillary items required for efficient operations and anticipates commencing operations
soon.</span></p>

<p style="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 27pt"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE DATED SEPTEMBER 14, 2023
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Zion
Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. Announces Award of New Megiddo Valleys License 434 Allowing for Ongoing Oil And Gas Exploration in Israel</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Re-Completion
Operations in the Megiddo-Jezreel #1 Well (MJ-01) to move forward.</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">DALLAS
and CAESAREA, Israel, September 14, 2023 /PRNewswire/ -- Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. (OTCQX: ZNOG) is excited to announce that the State
of Israel has awarded Zion a new exploration license, named the Megiddo Valleys #434.<BR>
<BR></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&quot;Today
marks a significant milestone for Zion Oil &amp; Gas, and we are thankful to our persevering shareholders and supporters,&quot; said
Zion Oil &amp; Gas CEO Rob Dunn. &ldquo;This license is a major endorsement from the State of Israel and affirms our longstanding commitment
to unlocking Israel&rsquo;s onshore energy potential.&rdquo;<BR>
<BR></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="A map of the middle east&#10;&#10;Description automatically generated" STYLE="height: 333px; width: 431px"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Approximate
boundaries of Zion&rsquo;s new exploration license area awarded on September 14, 2023.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">This
exploration license 434, similar to Zion&rsquo;s previous exploration licenses, will be valid for three years until September 13, 2026,
with the option of four 1-year extensions for a total of seven full years until September 13, 2030. This new license includes approximately
302 square kilometers or about 75,000 acres.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Zion
plans to start re-completion operations on the Megiddo-Jezreel #1 well (MJ-01) as soon as possible. Zion is deploying new technologies,
focusing on new stimulation methods for MJ-01, and aiming to potentially unlock hydrocarbon flows in several identified key zones. Zion
has already procured service contractors and ancillary items required for efficient operations and anticipates commencing operations
in Q4.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"></FONT></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1; Value: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->1<!-- Field: /Sequence -->&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Zion attributes these achievements to God&rsquo;s faithful provision through the unwavering support of its shareholders and steadfast
prayers for Zion Oil &amp; Gas.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&quot;We&rsquo;ve
had to wait patiently for this license, and God uses times of waiting to prepare His people for greater things,&rdquo; said Zion Oil
&amp; Gas Founder John Brown. &ldquo;We know that our trust in God will never be without reward according to His Plans.&quot;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
Zion Oil &amp; Gas</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Zion
Oil &amp; Gas, a US public company traded on the OTC Market, explores for oil and gas onshore in Israel.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Investments
can be made directly and without brokerage fees or commissions via Zion&rsquo;s website at <U>www.zionoil.com</U> through Zion&rsquo;s
Direct Stock Purchase Program.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&ldquo;<FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Blessed
is the one who perseveres under trial because, having stood the test, that person will receive the crown of life that the Lord has promised
to those who love him.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">James
1:12</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;To

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;The

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;Sing

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Isaiah
